                </template>      <template id="partials" pattern="(\s+\S+)&#123;2&#125;\s+\d+(\s+\S+)&#123;2&#125;\s*" endPattern="(\s+\S+)&#123;2&#125;\s+\d+(\s+\S+)&#123;2&#125;\s*" endPattern2="~" repeat="*">        <record repeat="1" />        <templateList>          <template pattern=".*" endPattern=".*" endPattern2="~" repeat="*">            <record>&#123;F,v:dosenergy&#125;&#123;1_33E,v:spin&#125;</record>            <transform process="split" xpath=".//cml:array[@dictRef='v:spin']" dictRef="v:spin" />            <transform process="createArray" xpath="." from=".//cml:scalar[@dictRef='v:spin'][position() mod 2 = 1]" dictRef="v:spin1" />            <transform process="createArray" xpath="." from=".//cml:scalar[@dictRef='v:spin']" dictRef="v:spin2" />
